                  type="button"

                >
                  Subscribe
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="container">
          <div className="copyright">
            <div className="row">
              <div className="col-md-6 text-center text-md-start mb-3 mb-md-0">

                </a>
                , All rights reserved.
              </div>
              <div className="col-md-6 text-center text-md-end">
                <div className="footer-menu">
                  <a href="#">Home</a>
                  <a href="#">Cookies</a>
                  <a href="#">Help</a>
                  <a href="#">FAQs</a>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </>
  );
}

                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

                  OnLearny
                </a>
                , All rights reserved.
              </div>
              <div className="col-md-6 text-center text-md-end">
                <div className="footer-menu">
                  <a href="#">Home</a>
                  <a href="#">Cookies</a>
                  <a href="#">Help</a>
                  <a href="#">FAQs</a>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </>
  );
}
